 mukhid ne apane letters head par likh kar diya tha ki vah sadik khan ko 10 saal se jaanate hai or vah acha ladkaa he
 The police has now arrested former councilor Mukhid on the charge of giving false information

 But still the condition of Ganga seems to be the same
 desh main 2,071 kilometre kshetra main bahane valindiganga ke bare main world wildlife fund (world Wildlife Fund) kaa kahana he ki ganga vishwa kii sabase adhik sankatagrast nadiyon main se ek he kyonki lagbhag sabhi duusari bhartiya nadiyon kii tarah ganga main lagaataar pehle baadh or phir sookhe kii sthiti paidaa ho rahi he
 From the Himalayas in the Uttarakhand to the Sundarbans of the Bay of Bengal, the Ganges irrigates vast tracts
 ganga bharat main 2,071 kimi or uske baad bangladesh main apni sahaayak nadiyon ke saath 10 lakh varg kilometre kshetrafal ke ati vishaal upjau maidan kii rachana karti he
 The states en route to the Ganges include Uttarakhand, Uttar Pradesh, Bihar, Jharkhand and West Bengal
 ganga main uttar kii ore se aakar milane vaali pramukh sahaayak nadiyon main yamuna, ramganga, karnaali (ghaghara), tapti, gandak, kosi or kakshi hai jabaki dakshin ke pathaar se aakar milane vaali pramukh nadiyon main chambal, son, betwa, ken, dakshini tose aadi shaamil hai
 Yamuna is the most important tributary of the Ganges, which originates from the Yamunotri glacier of Bandar Punch peak of the Himalayas
 ganga uttarakhand main 110 kimi, uttar pradesh main 1,450 kilometre, bihar main 445 kimi or pashchim bengal main 520 kimi kaa safar tay karte hue bengal kii khadi main milti he
 Spiritual significance of Ganga
 
 
 hamaare granthon main ganga kaa aadhyatmik or saanskrithik mahatv bhi he
 According to the texts, Ganga means flowing
 ganga bharat kii pahchaan he or desh ke aadhyatmik tathaa saanskrithik mulyon ko pirone vaali ek moolbhoot door bhi he

 Indian Space agency-isro is going to launch INSAT-3DR through GSLV today, taking important steps forward in the field of meteorology
 ye ek wedar satellite he or ise sriharikota ke satish dhawan spes centre se guuruuvaar shaam 4 bajkar 10 minute par launch kiya jayega
 This will be the tenth flight of India's geosynchronous satellite launch vehicle and the flight has been named GSLV-F05
 jieselvi-epa05 ke jariye 2211 kilogram vajan ke inset-3 diaar satellite ko jeeosteshnari transfar orbit main launch kiya jayega
 The INSAT-3DR satellite will install itself in the final orbit using its rocket system after being placed in the geostationary transfer orbit
 jieselvi-epa05 kii udaan main desh main banaae gaye cryogenic apper stage (siues) ingine kaa istemaal kiya jayega
 This would be gslv's first operational flight using cryogenic upper stage
 jieselvi-epa05 ko teenon stages ke liye plan kiya gaya he
 Best Imaging System and Advance System INSAT-3DR is a state-of-the-art weather satellite, equipped with the best imaging system and atmospheric sounder
 vaise to mausam kii jaankaree ke liye teen satellite kalpana-1, inset-3e or inset-3di pehle se hi jeeosteshnari orbit main gum rahe hai or mausam kii sateek jaankaree vibhaag ko de rahe hai
 But INSAT-3DR is advanced in all respects from these three satellites
 40 staron par vayumandal kaa taapmaana maapne main sakshamkalpana-1 or inset-3e main aise imaging system hai jo visibil, niyar-infrared, shortwave infrared, water vaipar or thermal infrared band main imaging kar sakate hai
 The INSAT-3D Satellite Atomospheric Sounding System launched in 2013 is installed
 is system ke jariye inset-3di jameen se 70 kilometre tak kii oonchai tak 40 staron par vayumandal katapamanaur 15 kilometre kii oonchai tak 21 staron par nami kaa level sahi sahi naap saktaa he
 Dependence on foreign agencies will reduce
 INSAT-3DR is an advanced version of satellite inset-3d
 inset 3 diaar satellite middle infrared band kii imaging karne kii kshamta se las he or isse raat ke vakt bhi badalon or kohre kii sateek jaankaree mil sakegi
 These satellites will be able to give accurate data of sea surface temperature through imaging in two thermal infrared bands
 isse videshi agenciyon par bharat ke mausam vibhaag kii nirbharta kaaphi had tak ghat jaaegi
 In addition to these features, INSAT-3DR is also equipped with a data relay transponder as well as a search and rescue transponder
 isse kisi aapadaa ke vakt logon ko dhundhakar bachaane main madad milegi
